onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="8-bit
(band)">8-Bit</a>
and
Paza
on
<i><a
href="/wiki/Hell_Yes_(EP)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Hell
Yes
(EP)">Hell
Yes</a></i>,
an
<a
href="/wiki/Extended_play?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Extended
play">EP</a>
issued
in
February
2005.<sup
id="cite_ref-guerolito_47-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-guerolito-47"><span>[</span>47<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
December
2005,
Geffen
also
issued
<i><a
href="/wiki/Guerolito?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Guerolito">Guerolito</a></i>,
a
fully
reworked
version
of
<i>Guero</i>
featuring
remixes
by
the
<a
href="/wiki/Beastie_Boys?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Beastie
Boys">Beastie
Boys</a>'
<a
href="/wiki/Ad-Rock?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Ad-Rock">Ad-Rock</a>,
the
Dust
Brothers'
<a
href="/wiki/John_King_(producer)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="John
King
(producer)">John
King</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Scotland?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Scotland">Scottish</a>
electronic
duo
<a
href="/wiki/Boards_of_Canada?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Boards
of
Canada">Boards
of
Canada</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-guerolito_47-2"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-guerolito-47"><span>[</span>47<span>]</span></a></sup>
<i>Guerolito</i>
combines
remixes
previously
heard
as
B-sides
and
new
versions
of
album
tracks
to
make
a
track-by-track
reconfiguration
of
the
album.<sup
id="cite_ref-guerolito_47-3"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-guerolito-47"><span>[</span>47<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p><i><a
href="/wiki/The_Information?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Information">The
Information</a></i>,
Beck's
ninth
studio
album,
began
production
around
the
same
time
as
<i>Guero</i>,
in
2003.
Working
with
producer
Nigel
Godrich,
Beck
built
a
studio
in
his
garden,
where
they
wrote
many
of
the
tracks.<sup
id="cite_ref-rs06_51-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-rs06-51"><span>[</span>51<span>]</span></a></sup>
&quot;The
idea
was
to
get
people
in
a
room
together
recording
live,
hitting
bad
notes
and
screaming,&quot;
said
Beck,
adding
that
the
album
is
best
described
as
&quot;introspective
hip
hop&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-rs06.1_52-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-rs06.1-52"><span>[</span>52<span>]</span></a></sup>
Beck
described
the
recording
process
as
&quot;painful&quot;,
noting
that
he
edited
down
songs
constantly
and
he
perhaps
recorded
the
album
three
times.<sup
id="cite_ref-bbc_53-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-bbc-53"><span>[</span>53<span>]</span></a></sup>
For
the
release,
Beck
was
allowed
for
the
first
time
to
fulfill
a
long-running
wish
for
an
unconventional
rollout:
he
made
low-budget
videos
to
accompany
each
song,
packaged
the
CD
with
sheets
of
stickers
so
buyers
could
customize
the
cover,
and
leaked
tracks
and
videos
on
his
website
months
ahead
of
the
album's
release.<sup
id="cite_ref-rs06_51-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-rs06-51"><span>[</span>51<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-54"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-54"><span>[</span>54<span>]</span></a></sup>
Digital
download
releases
automatically
downloaded
the
song's
additional
video
for
each
single
sale,
and
physical
copies
came
bundled
with
an
additional
DVD
featuring
fifteen
videos.<sup
id="cite_ref-rs06_51-2"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-rs06-51"><span>[</span>51<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<h3><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Modern_Guilt.2C_Song_Reader_and_independent_production_work_.282008.E2.80.9312.29"><i>Modern
Guilt</i>,
<i>Song
Reader</i>
and
independent
production
work
(2008–12)</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Beck&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9"
title="Edit
section:
Modern
Guilt,
Song
Reader
and
independent
production
work
(2008–12)">edit</a>]</span></h3>








<p>In
2007,
Beck
released
the
single
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Timebomb_(Beck_song)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Timebomb
(Beck
song)">Timebomb</a>&quot;,
which
was
nominated
for
a
<a
href="/wiki/Grammy_Award?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Grammy
Award">Grammy
Award</a>
for
Best
Solo
Rock
Vocal
Performance.<sup
id="cite_ref-nyt08_55-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-nyt08-55"><span>[</span>55<span>]</span></a></sup>
For
his
next
studio
effort,
his
tenth,
Beck
tapped
<a
href="/wiki/Danger_Mouse?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Danger
Mouse">Danger
Mouse</a>
to
produce,
and
the
two
first
met
in
December
2007
to
record.
The
duo
knocked
out
two
tracks
in
two
days,
but
the
notion
that
the
album
would
be
finished
in
a
timely
fashion
soon
evaporated.<sup
id="cite_ref-nyt08_55-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-nyt08-55"><span>[</span>55<span>]</span></a></sup>
Beck
had
known
Danger
Mouse
casually
before,
as
many
of
his
former
musicians
ended
up
working
with
Danger
Mouse's
side
project,
<a
href="/wiki/Gnarls_Barkley?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Gnarls
Barkley">Gnarls
Barkley</a>.
Still,
the
musicians
were
surprised
at
how
well
they
got
along.<sup
id="cite_ref-rs08_56-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-rs08-56"><span>[</span>56<span>]</span></a></sup>
Following
the
grueling
recording
schedule,
Beck
was
exhausted,
calling
it
&quot;the
most
intense
work
I've
ever
done
on
anything&quot;,
relating
that
he
&quot;did
at
least
10
weeks
with
no
days
off,
until
four
or
five
in
the
morning
every
night.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-rs08_56-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-rs08-56"><span>[</span>56<span>]</span></a></sup>
Beck's
original
vision
was
a
short
10-track
burst
with
two-minute
songs,
but
the
songs
gradually
grew
as
he
fit
'two
years
of
songwriting
into
two
and
a
half
months.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-rs08_56-2"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-rs08-56"><span>[</span>56<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p><i><a
href="/wiki/Modern_Guilt?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Modern
Guilt">Modern
Guilt</a></i>
(2008),
&quot;full
of
off-kilter
rhythms
and
left-field
breakdowns,
with
an
overall
1960s
vibe&quot;,
was
the
final
release
in
his
contract
with
Geffen
Records.
Beck,
then
38,
had
held
the
contract
since
his
early
20s.<sup
id="cite_ref-nyt08_55-2"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-nyt08-55"><span>[</span>55<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-rs08_56-3"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-rs08-56"><span>[</span>56<span>]</span></a></sup>
Released
from
his
label
contract
and
going
independent,
Beck
began
working
more
heavily
on
his
own
seven-year-old
label,
which
went
through
a
variety
of
names.<sup
id="cite_ref-p4k11_27-8"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-p4k11-27"><span>[</span>27<span>]</span></a></sup>
His
focus
on
smaller,
more
quixotic
projects,<sup
id="cite_ref-nym12_13-4"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-nym12-13"><span>[</span>13<span>]</span></a></sup>
Beck
moonlighted
as
a
producer,
working
with
artists
such
as
<a
href="/wiki/Charlotte_Gainsbourg?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Charlotte
Gainsbourg">Charlotte
Gainsbourg</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Thurston_Moore?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Thurston
Moore">Thurston
Moore</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Stephen_Malkmus?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Stephen
Malkmus">Stephen
Malkmus</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-p4k11_27-9"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-p4k11-27"><span>[</span>27<span>]</span></a></sup>
He
worked
for
five
or
six
days
a
week
at
the
small
studio
on
his
property
in
Malibu,<sup
id="cite_ref-nym12_13-5"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-nym12-13"><span>[</span>13<span>]</span></a></sup>
and
founded
<a
href="/wiki/Record_Club?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Record
Club">Record
Club</a>,
a
project
whereby
an
entire
classic
album—by
<a
href="/wiki/The_Velvet_Underground?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Velvet
Underground">The
Velvet
Underground</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Leonard_Cohen?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Leonard
Cohen">Leonard
Cohen</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/INXS?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="INXS">INXS</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Yanni?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Yanni">Yanni</a>—would
be
covered
by
another
singer
in
the
span
of
a
single
day.<sup
id="cite_ref-nym12_13-6"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-nym12-13"><span>[</span>13<span>]</span></a></sup>
Beck
provided
four
songs
for
the
film
<i><a
href="/wiki/Scott_Pilgrim_vs._the_World?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Scott
Pilgrim
vs.
the
World">Scott
Pilgrim
vs.
the
World</a></i>
(2010),
each
attributed
to
the
title
character's
fictional
band,
Sex
Bob-Omb.<sup
id="cite_ref-ew10_57-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-ew10-57"><span>[</span>57<span>]</span></a></sup>
Beck
also
collaborated
with
<a
href="/wiki/Philip_Glass?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Philip
Glass">Philip
Glass</a>,<sup
id="cite_ref-collabglass_58-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-collabglass-58"><span>[</span>58<span>]</span></a></sup>
<a
href="/wiki/Jack_White_(musician)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Jack
White
(musician)"
class="mw-redirect">Jack
White</a>,<sup
id="cite_ref-collabwhite_59-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-collabwhite-59"><span>[</span>59<span>]</span></a></sup>
<a
href="/wiki/Tobacco_(musician)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Tobacco
(musician)">Tobacco</a>
of
<a
href="/wiki/Black_Moth_Super_Rainbow?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Black
Moth
Super
Rainbow">Black
Moth
Super
Rainbow</a>,<sup
id="cite_ref-collab1_60-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-collab1-60"><span>[</span>60<span>]</span></a></sup>
Jamie
Lidell,<sup
id="cite_ref-collab2_61-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-collab2-61"><span>[</span>61<span>]</span></a></sup>
<a
href="/wiki/Seu_Jorge?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Seu
Jorge">Seu
Jorge</a>,<sup
id="cite_ref-collab3_62-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-collab3-62"><span>[</span>62<span>]</span></a></sup>
<a
href="/wiki/Childish_Gambino?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Childish
Gambino"
class="mw-redirect">Childish
Gambino</a>,<sup
id="cite_ref-collab5_63-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-collab5-63"><span>[</span>63<span>]</span></a></sup>
and
<a
href="/wiki/The_Lonely_Island?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Lonely
Island">The
Lonely
Island</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-collab6_64-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-collab6-64"><span>[</span>64<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p><i><a
href="/wiki/Song_Reader?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Song
Reader">Song
Reader</a></i>,
a
project
Beck
released
in
December
2012,
is
20
songs
presented
only
as
sheet
music,
in
the
hopes
that
enterprising
musicians
will
record
their
own
versions.<sup
id="cite_ref-srnpr_65-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-srnpr-65"><span>[</span>65<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
idea
of
<i>Song
Reader</i>
came
about
nearly
fifteen
years
prior,
shortly
after
the
release
of
<i><a
href="/wiki/Odelay?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Odelay">Odelay</a></i>.<sup
id="cite_ref-nym12_13-7"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-nym12-13"><span>[</span>13<span>]</span></a></sup>
When
sent
a
book
of
transcribed
sheet
music
for
that
album,
Beck
decided
to
play
through
it
and
grew
interested
in
the
world
before
recorded
sound.
He
aimed
to
keep
the
arrangements
as
open
as
possible,
to
re-create
the
simplicity
of
the
standards,
and
became
preoccupied
with
creating
only
pieces
that
could
fit
within
the
<a
href="/wiki/Great_American_Songbook?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Great
American
Songbook">Great
American
Songbook</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-nym12_13-8"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-nym12-13"><span>[</span>13<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
2013
Beck
began
playing
special
<i><a
href="/wiki/Song_Reader?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Song
Reader">Song
Reader</a></i>
concerts
with
a
variety
of
guests
and
announced
he
was
working
on
a
record
of
<i><a
href="/wiki/Song_Reader?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Song
Reader">Song
Reader</a></i>
material
with
other
musicians
as
well
as
possibly
a
compilation
of
fan
versions.<sup
id="cite_ref-Future_Heart_66-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Future_Heart-66"><span>[</span>66<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<h3><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Eleventh_and_twelfth_studio_albums_.282013.E2.80.93present.29">Eleventh
and
twelfth
studio
albums
(2013–present)</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Beck&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10"
title="Edit
section:
Eleventh
and
twelfth
studio
albums
(2013–present)">edit</a>]</span></h3>








<p>In
the
summer
of
2013,
Beck
was
reported
to
be
working
on
two
new
studio
albums:
one
a
more
self-contained
acoustic
disc
in
the
vein
of
<i>One
Foot
in
the
Grave</i>
and
another
described
as
a
&quot;proper
follow-up&quot;
to
<i>Modern
Guilt</i>.<sup
id="cite_ref-rs13_67-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-rs13-67"><span>[</span>67<span>]</span></a></sup>
Beck
expects
to
release
both
albums
independently.
He
released
two
standalone
singles
over
the
course
of
the
summer:
the
<a
href="/wiki/Electro_music?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Electro
music"
class="mw-redirect">electro</a>
ballad
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Defriended?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Defriended">Defriended</a>&quot;
and
the
chorus-heavy
&quot;I
Won't
Be
Long&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-rs13_67-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-rs13-67"><span>[</span>67<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-rs13.1_68-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-rs13.1-68"><span>[</span>68<span>]</span></a></sup>
A
third
single,
&quot;Gimme&quot;,
appeared
on
September
17.<sup
id="cite_ref-69"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-69"><span>[</span>69<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
October
2013,
it
was
announced
that
Beck
signed
to
Capitol
Records.
Beck
released
his
twelfth
studio
album
entitled
<i><a
href="/wiki/Morning_Phase?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Morning
Phase">Morning
Phase</a></i>
on
21
February
2014.<sup
id="cite_ref-Morning_Phase_Amazon_70-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Morning_Phase_Amazon-70"><span>[</span>70<span>]</span></a></sup>
For
the
recording
of
<i>Morning
Phase</i>,
Beck
reunited
with
many
of
the
same
musicians
with
whom
he
had
worked
on
the
critically
acclaimed
2002
album
<i><a
href="/wiki/Sea_Change_(album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Sea
Change
(album)">Sea
Change</a></i>.<sup
id="cite_ref-71"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-71"><span>[</span>71<span>]</span></a></sup>
On
January
20,
2014,
the
album's
first
single
&quot;Blue
Moon&quot;
was
released.<sup
id="cite_ref-Blue_Moon_Amazon_72-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Blue_Moon_Amazon-72"><span>[</span>72<span>]</span></a></sup>
Beck
released
the
second
single
from
the
album
on
February
4,
2014.<sup
id="cite_ref-Waking_Light_Amazon_73-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Waking_Light_Amazon-73"><span>[</span>73<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-74"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-74"><span>[</span>74<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Collaborations_and_contributions">Collaborations
and
contributions</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Beck&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11"
title="Edit
section:
Collaborations
and
contributions">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<p>In
1999,
Beck
contributed
to
a
tribute
album
for
<a
href="/wiki/Bruce_Haack?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Bruce
Haack">Bruce
Haack</a>
and
Esther
Nelson
and
their
label
Dimension
5
Records.
The
album,
<a
href="/wiki/Dimension_Mix?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Dimension
Mix">Dimension
Mix</a>,
released
in
2005,
was
a
benefit
for
<a
href="/wiki/Cure_Autism_Now?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Cure
Autism
Now"
class="mw-redirect">Cure
Autism
Now</a>
that
was
produced
by
<a
href="/wiki/Ross_Harris_(actor)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Ross
Harris
(actor)">Ross
Harris</a>,
an
early
collaborator
who
designed
the
artwork
for
&quot;Mellow
Gold&quot;.</p>








<p>On
June
18,
2009,
Beck
announced
that
he
was
starting
an
experiment
called
<a
href="/wiki/Record_Club?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Record
Club">Record
Club</a>,
in
which
he
and
other
musicians
would
record
cover
versions
of
entire
albums
in
one
day.
The
first
album
covered
by
Beck's
Record
Club
was
<i><a
href="/wiki/The_Velvet_Underground_%26_Nico?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Velvet
Underground
&amp;
Nico">The
Velvet
Underground
&amp;
Nico</a></i>.
Starting
on
June
18,
the
club
began
posting
covers
of
songs
from
the
album
on
Thursday
evenings,
each
with
its
own
video.<sup
id="cite_ref-75"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-75"><span>[</span>75<span>]</span></a></sup>
On
September
4,
2009,
Beck
announced
the
second
Record
Club
album,
<i><a
href="/wiki/Songs_of_Leonard_Cohen?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Songs
of
Leonard
Cohen">Songs
of
Leonard
Cohen</a></i>.
Contributors
included
<a
href="/wiki/MGMT?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="MGMT">MGMT</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Devendra_Banhart?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Devendra
Banhart">Devendra
Banhart</a>,
Andrew
Stockdale
of
<a
href="/wiki/Wolfmother?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Wolfmother">Wolfmother</a>
and
Binki
Shapiro
of
<a
href="/wiki/Little_Joy?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Little
Joy">Little
Joy</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-76"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-76"><span>[</span>76<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
the
third
Record
Club
venture,
<a
href="/wiki/Wilco?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Wilco">Wilco</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Feist_(singer)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Feist
(singer)">Feist</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Jamie_Lidell?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Jamie
Lidell">Jamie
Lidell</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/James_Gadson?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="James
Gadson">James
Gadson</a>
joined
Beck
to
cover
<a
href="/wiki/Skip_Spence?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Skip
Spence">Skip
Spence</a>'s
<a
href="/wiki/Oar_(Skip_Spence_album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Oar
(Skip
Spence
album)"
class="mw-redirect"><i>Oar</i></a>.
The
first
song,
&quot;Little
Hands&quot;,
was
posted
on
Beck's
website
on
November
12,
2009.<sup
id="cite_ref-77"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-77"><span>[</span>77<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
Record
Club
has
since
covered
albums
by
<a
href="/wiki/INXS?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="INXS">INXS</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Yanni?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Yanni">Yanni</a>.</p>








<p>On
June
19,
2009,
Beck
announced
Planned
Obsolescence,
a
weekly
DJ
set
put
together
by
Beck
or
guest
DJs.
Soon
after,
on
July
7,
Beck
announced
that
his
website
would
be
featuring
&quot;extended
informal
conversations
with
musicians,
artists,
filmmakers,
and
other
various
persons&quot;
in
a
section
called
Irrelevant
Topics.
Then,
on
July
12,
he
added
a
section
called
Videotheque,
which
he
said
would
contain
&quot;promotional
videos
from
each
album,
as
well
as
live
clips,
TV
show
appearances
and
other
rarities&quot;.</p>








<p>Also
in
2009,
Beck
collaborated
with
<a
href="/wiki/Charlotte_Gainsbourg?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Charlotte
Gainsbourg">Charlotte
Gainsbourg</a>
on
her
album
<i><a
href="/wiki/IRM_(album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="IRM
(album)">IRM</a></i>,
which
was
released
in
January
2010.
Beck
wrote
the
music,
co-wrote
the
lyrics,
and
produced
and
mixed
the
album.
The
lead
single,
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Heaven_Can_Wait_(Charlotte_Gainsbourg_song)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Heaven
Can
Wait
(Charlotte
Gainsbourg
song)">Heaven
Can
Wait</a>&quot;,
is
a
duet
by
Beck
and
Gainsbourg.<sup
id="cite_ref-78"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-78"><span>[</span>78<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
late
February
2010,
it
was
announced
that
electronic
artist
<a
href="/wiki/Tobacco_(musician)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Tobacco
(musician)">Tobacco</a>
of
<a
href="/wiki/Black_Moth_Super_Rainbow?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Black
Moth
Super
Rainbow">Black
Moth
Super
Rainbow</a>
had
collaborated
with
Beck
on
two
songs,
&quot;Fresh
Hex&quot;
and
&quot;Grape
Aerosmith&quot;,
on
his
upcoming
album
<i>Maniac
Meat</i>.
Tobacco
revealed
that
in
making
the
album,
Beck
sent
the
vocal
parts
to
him,
and
that
they
had
never
actually
met.<sup
class="Template-Fact"
style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a
href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed"
target="_blank"
title="Wikipedia:Citation
needed"><span
title="This
claim
needs
references
to
reliable
sources.
(May
2010)">citation
needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>








<p>In
March
2010,
Beck
revealed
that
he
had
produced
songs
for
the
new
Jamie
Lidell
album,
<i><a
href="/wiki/Compass_(Jamie_Lidell_album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Compass
(Jamie
Lidell
album)">Compass</a></i>.<sup
id="cite_ref-79"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-79"><span>[</span>79<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
the
summer
of
2010,
Beck
contributed
songs
to
both
<i><a
href="/wiki/The_Twilight_Saga:_Eclipse_(soundtrack)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Twilight
Saga:
Eclipse
(soundtrack)">The
Twilight
Saga:
Eclipse</a></i>
soundtrack,
with
&quot;Let's
Get
Lost&quot;
(a
duet
with
<a
href="/wiki/Bat_for_Lashes?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Bat
for
Lashes">Bat
for
Lashes</a>),
and
<i><a
href="/wiki/True_Blood?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="True
Blood">True
Blood</a>
(HBO
Original
Series
Soundtrack,
Vol.
2)</i>,
with
&quot;Bad
Blood&quot;.
He
also
contributed
songs
to
the
soundtrack
of
the
movie
<i><a
href="/wiki/Scott_Pilgrim_vs._the_World?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Scott
Pilgrim
vs.
the
World">Scott
Pilgrim
vs.
the
World</a></i>,
which
was
released
in
August
2010.
Two
of
the
songs
that
Beck
specifically
wrote
for
the
film
appeared
in
its
theatrical
trailer.</p>








<p>In
2011,
he
collaborated
with
<a
href="/wiki/Seu_Jorge?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Seu
Jorge">Seu
Jorge</a>
on
a
track
titled
&quot;Tropic&aacute;lia
(Mario
C.
2011
Remix)&quot;
for
the
<a
href="/wiki/Red_Hot_Organization?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Red
Hot
Organization">Red
Hot
Organization's</a>
most
recent
charitable
album
<i>Red
Hot+Rio
2.</i>
The
album
is
a
follow-up
to
the
1996
<i><a
href="/wiki/Red_Hot_%2B_Rio?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Red
Hot
+
Rio">Red
Hot
+
Rio</a>.</i>
Proceeds
from
the
sales
will
be
donated
to
raise
awareness
and
money
to
fight
AIDS/HIV
and
related
health
and
social
issues.<sup
id="cite_ref-tracklisting_80-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-tracklisting-80"><span>[</span>80<span>]</span></a></sup>
He
also
contributed
on
the
song
&quot;Attracted
to
Us&quot;
on
<i><a
href="/wiki/Turtleneck_%26_Chain?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Turtleneck
&amp;
Chain">Turtleneck
&amp;
Chain</a></i>,
the
newest
album
from
<a
href="/wiki/The_Lonely_Island?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Lonely
Island">The
Lonely
Island</a>.</p>








<p>Also
in
2011,
Beck
produced
a
solo
album
by
<a
href="/wiki/Thurston_Moore?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Thurston
Moore">Thurston
Moore</a>
of
<a
href="/wiki/Sonic_Youth?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Sonic
Youth">Sonic
Youth</a>
called
<i><a
href="/wiki/Demolished_Thoughts?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Demolished
Thoughts">Demolished
Thoughts</a></i>.
An
album
he
produced
for
<a
href="/wiki/Stephen_Malkmus_and_the_Jicks?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Stephen
Malkmus
and
the
Jicks">Stephen
Malkmus
and
the
Jicks</a>,
<i>Mirror
Traffic</i>,
was
released
in
August
2011.</p>








<p>In
October
2011,
it
was
widely
reported
that
Beck
and
producer
Hector
Castillo
were
collaborating
with
American
composer
<a
href="/wiki/Philip_Glass?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Philip
Glass">Philip
Glass</a>
to
produce
a
remix
album
of
the
composer's
works
in
honor
of
his
75th
birthday.<sup
id="cite_ref-81"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-81"><span>[</span>81<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-82"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-82"><span>[</span>82<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-83"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-83"><span>[</span>83<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-84"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-84"><span>[</span>84<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
album,
<i>Rework
Philip
Glass
Remixed</i>,
was
released
on
October
23,
2012,
to
critical
acclaim,
and
featured
Beck
as
both
a
curator
and
a
performer.<sup
id="cite_ref-85"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-85"><span>[</span>85<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-86"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-86"><span>[</span>86<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
particular,
Pitchfork
described
Beck's
22-minute
contribution
to
the
album,
&quot;NYC:
73-78&quot;,
as
&quot;a
fantasia
...
the
most
startling
and
original
piece
of
music
with
Beck's
name
on
it
in
a
while,
and
the
first
new
work
to
bear
his
own
spirit
in
even
longer.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-87"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-87"><span>[</span>87<span>]</span></a></sup>
Reflecting
on
Beck's
contribution
to
the
album,
Glass
remarked
that
he
was
&quot;impressed
by
the
novelty
and
freshness
of
a
lot
of
the
ideas&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-88"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-88"><span>[</span>88<span>]</span></a></sup>
Beyond
his
work
as
a
performer,
Beck
acted
as
the
album's
curator,
bringing
together
a
diverse
collection
of
artists—including
<a
href="/wiki/Amon_Tobin?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Amon
Tobin">Amon
Tobin</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Tyondai_Braxton?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Tyondai
Braxton">Tyondai
Braxton</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Nosaj_Thing?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Nosaj
Thing">Nosaj
Thing</a>,
and
<a
href="/wiki/Memory_Tapes?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Memory
Tapes">Memory
Tapes</a>—whose
work
had
also
been
influenced
by
Glass.<sup
id="cite_ref-89"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-89"><span>[</span>89<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-90"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-90"><span>[</span>90<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
December
2012,
an
interactive
<a
href="/wiki/IPhone_app?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="IPhone
app"
class="mw-redirect">iPhone
app</a>
titled
&quot;Rework_&quot;
was
released
to
complement
the
album.<sup
id="cite_ref-91"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-91"><span>[</span>91<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-92"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-92"><span>[</span>92<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>Beck
has
contributed
three
new
songs—&quot;Cities&quot;,
&quot;Touch
the
People&quot;
and
&quot;Spiral
Staircase&quot;—to
the
PlayStation
3
and
PlayStation
Vita
Sound
Shapes,
which
is
now
available
for
purchase.<sup
class="Template-Fact"
style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a
href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed"
target="_blank"
title="Wikipedia:Citation
needed"><span
title="This
claim
needs
references
to
reliable
sources.
(July
2012)">citation
needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>








<p>Beck
collaborated
on
two
songs
for
<a
href="/wiki/Childish_Gambino?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Childish
Gambino"
class="mw-redirect">Childish
Gambino's</a>
&quot;Royalty&quot;
mixtape
in
2012.<sup
id="cite_ref-93"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-93"><span>[</span>93<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Musical_style">Musical
style</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Beck&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12"
title="Edit
section:
Musical
style">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<p>Beck's
musical
style
has
been
considered
alternative<sup
id="cite_ref-94"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-94"><span>[</span>94<span>]</span></a></sup>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Independent_music?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Independent
music">indie</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-95"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-95"><span>[</span>95<span>]</span></a></sup>
He
has
played
many
of
the
instruments
in
his
music
himself.<sup
id="cite_ref-the_information_96-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-the_information-96"><span>[</span>96<span>]</span></a></sup>
Beck
has
also
done
some
remixes
for
fellow
artists,
notably
<a
href="/wiki/David_Bowie?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="David
Bowie">David
Bowie</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Bj%C3%B6rk?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Bj&ouml;rk">Bj&ouml;rk</a>.
He
has
been
known
to
synthesize
several
musical
elements
together
in
his
music,
including
<a
href="/wiki/Folk_music?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Folk
music">folk</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Psychedelia?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Psychedelia">psychedelia</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Electronic_music?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Electronic
music">electronic</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Country_music?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Country
music">country</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Latin_American_music?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Latin
American
music">Latin
music</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Hip_hop_music?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Hip
hop
music">hip
hop</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Funk?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Funk">funk</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Soul_music?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Soul
music">soul</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Blues?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Blues">blues</a>,
and
many
types
of
<a
href="/wiki/Rock_music?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Rock
music">rock</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-guero_97-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-guero-97"><span>[</span>97<span>]</span></a></sup>
He
has
also
taken
music
from
Los
Angeles
as
a
reference
point
in
his
songs.<sup
id="cite_ref-guero_97-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-guero-97"><span>[</span>97<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>Beck
has
an
irreverent
style
of
<a
href="/wiki/Sampling_(music)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Sampling
(music)">sampling</a>,
often
using
such
sources
as
obscure
films
to
splice
together
cuts
of
people
talking
in
the
background
of
his
music,
or
various
other
<a
href="/wiki/Found_object?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Found
object">found
sounds</a>
to
create
<a
href="/wiki/Sound_collage?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Sound
collage">sound
collages</a>
in
the
background
of
his
music.<sup
class="Template-Fact"
style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a
href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed"
target="_blank"
title="Wikipedia:Citation
needed"><span
title="This
claim
needs
references
to
reliable
sources.
(October
2012)">citation
needed</span></a></i>]</sup></p>








<p>Pitchfork
Media
applauded
<i>Midnite
Vultures</i>,
saying,
&quot;Beck
wonderfully
blends
<a
href="/wiki/Prince_(musician)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Prince
(musician)">Prince</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Talking_Heads?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Talking
Heads">Talking
Heads</a>,
<i><a
href="/wiki/Paul%27s_Boutique?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Paul's
Boutique">Paul's
Boutique</a></i>,
'<a
href="/wiki/Shake_Your_Bon-Bon?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Shake
Your
Bon-Bon">Shake
Your
Bon-Bon</a>',
and
<a
href="/wiki/Mathlete?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Mathlete">Mathlete</a>
on
<i>Midnite
Vultures</i>,
his
most
consistent
and
playful
album
yet.&quot;
The
review
continued
to
comment
on
Beck,
saying
that
his
mix
of
goofy
piety
and
ambiguous
intent
helped
the
album.<sup
id="cite_ref-98"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-98"><span>[</span>98<span>]</span></a></sup>
A
Beck
song
called
&quot;Harry
Partch&quot;,
a
tribute
to
the
composer
and
his
&quot;Corporeal&quot;
music,
employs
<a
href="/wiki/Harry_Partch?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Harry
Partch">Partch</a>'s
<a
href="/wiki/Harry_Partch%27s_43-tone_scale?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Harry
Partch's
43-tone
scale">43-tone
scale</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-99"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-99"><span>[</span>99<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Art_career">Art
career</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Beck&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13"
title="Edit
section:
Art
career">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<p>During
1998,
Beck's
art
collaborations
with
his
grandfather
Al
Hansen
were
featured
in
an
exhibition
titled
&quot;Beck
&amp;
Al
Hansen:
Playing
With
Matches&quot;,
which
showcased
solo
and
collaborative
<a
href="/wiki/Collage?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Collage">collage</a>,
assemblage,
<a
href="/wiki/Drawing?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Drawing">drawing</a>
and
poetry
works.<sup
id="cite_ref-100"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-100"><span>[</span>100<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
show
toured
from
the
<a
href="/wiki/Santa_Monica_Museum_of_Art?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Santa
Monica
Museum
of
Art">Santa
Monica
Museum
of
Art</a>
to
galleries
in
New
York
City
and
<a
href="/wiki/Winnipeg?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Winnipeg">Winnipeg</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Manitoba?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Manitoba">Manitoba</a>,
in
Canada.
A
catalog
of
the
show
was
published
by
Plug
In
Editions/Smart
Art
Press.<sup
id="cite_ref-101"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-101"><span>[</span>101<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Personal_life">Personal
life</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Beck&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14"
title="Edit
section:
Personal
life">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<p>Beck's
nine-year
relationship
with
designer
Leigh
Limon
and
their
subsequent
breakup
is
said
to
have
inspired
his
2002
album,
<i>Sea
Change</i>.<sup
id="cite_ref-Salon_102-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Salon-102"><span>[</span>102<span>]</span></a></sup>
He
wrote
most
of
the
songs
for
the
album
in
one
week
after
the
breakup.<sup
id="cite_ref-Time_103-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Time-103"><span>[</span>103<span>]</span></a></sup>
Beck
married
actress
<a
href="/wiki/Marissa_Ribisi?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Marissa
Ribisi">Marissa
Ribisi</a>,
the
twin
sister
of
actor
<a
href="/wiki/Giovanni_Ribisi?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Giovanni
Ribisi">Giovanni
Ribisi</a>,
in
April
2004,<sup
id="cite_ref-104"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-104"><span>[</span>104<span>]</span></a></sup>
shortly
before
the
birth
of
their
son,
Cosimo
Henri.<sup
id="cite_ref-Spin_105-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Spin-105"><span>[</span>105<span>]</span></a></sup>
Ribisi
gave
birth
to
their
daughter,
Tuesday,
in
2007.<sup
id="cite_ref-nyt08_55-3"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-nyt08-55"><span>[</span>55<span>]</span></a></sup>
Marissa
and
Giovanni
Ribisi
were
delivered
by
Beck's
mother,
<a
href="/wiki/Bibbe_Hansen?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Bibbe
Hansen">Bibbe
Hansen</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-Celebrific_106-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Celebrific-106"><span>[</span>106<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
November
2013
Beck
revealed
he
had
suffered
a
severe
injury
to
his
spine
a
few
years
earlier
but
was
now
doing
better.<sup
id="cite_ref-Future_Heart_66-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Future_Heart-66"><span>[</span>66<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<h3><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Scientology">Scientology</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Beck&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15"
title="Edit
section:
Scientology">edit</a>]</span></h3>








<p>Beck
has
been
involved
in
<a
href="/wiki/Scientology?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Scientology">Scientology</a>
for
most
of
his
life;
his
wife,
Marissa,
is
also
a
second-generation
Scientologist.<sup
id="cite_ref-Celebrific_106-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Celebrific-106"><span>[</span>106<span>]</span></a></sup>
Beck
publicly
acknowledged
his
affiliation
with
Scientology
for
the
first
time
in
an
interview
published
in
<i><a
href="/wiki/The_New_York_Times_Magazine?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
New
York
Times
Magazine">The
New
York
Times
Magazine</a></i>
on
March
6,
2005.
Further
confirmation
came
in
an
interview
with
the
Irish
<i><a
href="/wiki/Sunday_Tribune?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Sunday
Tribune">Sunday
Tribune's</a></i>
<i>i
Magazine</i>
on
June
11,
2005,
where
he
was
quoted
as
saying,
&quot;Yeah,
I'm
a
Scientologist.
My
father
has
been
a
Scientologist
for
about
35
years,
so
I
grew
up
in
and
around
it.&quot;
When
questioned
by
the
interviewer
about
Scientology's
core
beliefs,
he
replied:</p>








<blockquote>









<p>What
it
actually
is
is
just
sort
of,
uh,
you
know,
I
think
it's
about
philosophy
and
sort
of,
uh,
all
these
kinds
of,
you
know,
ideals
that
are
common
to
a
lot
of
religions....
There's
nothing
fantastical
...
just
a
real
deep
grassroots
concerted
effort
for
humanitarian
causes.
I
don't
know
if
you
know
the
stuff
they
have.
It's
unbelievable
the
stuff
they
are
doing.
Education
...
they
have
free
centres
all
over
the
place
for
poor
kids.
They
have
the
number
one
drug
rehabilitation
programme
in
the
entire
world
(called
<a
href="/wiki/Narconon?qsrc=3044#Narconon_and_Scientology"
title="Narconon">Narconon</a>).
It
has
a
90-something
percent
success
rate....
When
you
look
at
the
actual
facts
and
not
what's
conjured
in
people's
minds
that's
all
bullshit
to
me
because
I've
actually
seen
stuff
first
hand.<sup
id="cite_ref-Sunday_Tribune_107-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Sunday_Tribune-107"><span>[</span>107<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








</blockquote>








<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Appearances_in_media">Appearances
in
media</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Beck&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16"
title="Edit
section:
Appearances
in
media">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<p>The
1986
punk
rock
musical
film
<i><a
href="/wiki/Population:_1?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Population:
1">Population:
1</a></i>,
starring
<a
href="/wiki/Tomata_du_Plenty?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Tomata
du
Plenty">Tomata
du
Plenty</a>
of
<a
href="/wiki/The_Screamers?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Screamers">The
Screamers</a>,
features
a
young
Beck
in
a
small
nonspeaking
role.<sup
id="cite_ref-108"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-108"><span>[</span>108<span>]</span></a></sup>
Beck
also
appears
in
<i><a
href="/wiki/Southlander?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Southlander">Southlander</a></i>
(2001),
an
American
independent
film
by
Steve
Hanft
and
Ross
Harris.</p>








<p>In
1987
Beck
was
in
a
documentary
by
Sophie
Rachmuhl
that
features
young
poets
of
Los
Angeles.
This
film
was
released
only
to
local
theaters.
Rachmuhl
is
planning
a
re-release
of
this
film
on
DVD,
which
will
be
included
in
her
upcoming
book.<sup
id="cite_ref-109"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-109"><span>[</span>109<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>Beck
has
performed
on
<i><a
href="/wiki/Saturday_Night_Live?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Saturday
Night
Live">Saturday
Night
Live</a></i>
seven
times.
During
his
2006
performance
in
the
Hugh
Laurie
episode,
Beck
was
accompanied
by
the
puppets
that
had
been
used
onstage
during
his
world
tour.
He
has
made
two
cameo
appearances
as
himself
on
<i>Saturday
Night
Live</i>:
one
in
a
sketch
about
medicinal
marijuana,
and
one
in
a
VH1
<i><a
href="/wiki/Behind_the_Music?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Behind
the
Music">Behind
the
Music</a></i>
parody
that
featured
&quot;Fat
Albert
&amp;
the
Junkyard
Gang&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-110"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-110"><span>[</span>110<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>Beck
performed
a
guest
voice
as
himself
on
<a
href="/wiki/Matt_Groening?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Matt
Groening">Matt
Groening</a>'s
animated
show
<i><a
href="/wiki/Futurama?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Futurama">Futurama</a></i>,
in
the
episode
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Bendin%27_in_the_Wind?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Bendin'
in
the
Wind">Bendin'
in
the
Wind</a>&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-111"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-111"><span>[</span>111<span>]</span></a></sup>
He
performed
in
episode
11
of
the
fourth
season
of
<i><a
href="/wiki/The_Larry_Sanders_Show?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Larry
Sanders
Show">The
Larry
Sanders
Show</a></i>,
in
which
the
producer
character
<a
href="/wiki/List_of_characters_on_The_Larry_Sanders_Show?qsrc=3044#Artie"
title="List
of
characters
on
The
Larry
Sanders
Show"
class="mw-redirect">Artie</a>
(<a
href="/wiki/Rip_Torn?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Rip
Torn">Rip
Torn</a>)
referred
to
him
as
a
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Hillbilly?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Hillbilly">hillbilly</a>
from
outer
space&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-112"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-112"><span>[</span>112<span>]</span></a></sup>
He
also
made
a
very
brief
voice
appearance
in
the
1998
cartoon
feature
film
<i><a
href="/wiki/The_Rugrats_Movie?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Rugrats
Movie">The
Rugrats
Movie</a></i>,<sup
id="cite_ref-113"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-113"><span>[</span>113<span>]</span></a></sup>
and
guest-starred
as
himself
in
a
1997
episode
of
<i><a
href="/wiki/Space_Ghost_Coast_to_Coast?qsrc=3044"

title="Space
Ghost
Coast
to
Coast">Space
Ghost
Coast
to
Coast</a></i>
titled
&quot;Edelweiss&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-114"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-114"><span>[</span>114<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>Beck
has
also
made
appearances
on
the
Adult
Swim
show
<i><a
href="/wiki/Mission_Hill?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Mission
Hill">Mission
Hill</a></i>.
Accepting
an
award,
he
comes
up
onstage
wearing
the
new
&quot;Spicy
pants&quot;
trend.
In
consequence
the
main
character
begins
throwing
all
of
his
&quot;Beck&quot;
albums
out
his
upper-story
window.</p>








<p>In
an
episode
of
<i><a
href="/wiki/Celebrity_Deathmatch?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Celebrity
Deathmatch">Celebrity
Deathmatch</a></i>,
Beck
was
featured
fighting
Bj&ouml;rk
in
a
&quot;battle
to
be
the
best
monosyllabic
musician
of
all
time&quot;,
which
ended
with
both
of
them
slain
by
<a
href="/wiki/Johann_Sebastian_Bach?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Johann
Sebastian
Bach">Bach</a>,
who
appeared
via
a
time
machine.</p>








<p>On
January
22,
2010,
Beck
appeared
on
<i><a
href="/wiki/The_Tonight_Show_with_Conan_O%27Brien?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Tonight
Show
with
Conan
O'Brien">The
Tonight
Show
with
Conan
O'Brien</a>'</i>s
last
show
as
a
backup
guitarist
for
a
<a
href="/wiki/Will_Ferrell?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Will
Ferrell">Will
Ferrell</a>–led
rendition
of
<a
href="/wiki/Lynyrd_Skynyrd?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Lynyrd
Skynyrd">Lynyrd
Skynyrd</a>'s
&quot;<a
href="/wiki/Free_Bird?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Free
Bird">Free
Bird</a>&quot;
alongside
<a
href="/wiki/ZZ_Top?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="ZZ
Top">ZZ
Top</a>
guitarist
<a
href="/wiki/Billy_Gibbons?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Billy
Gibbons">Billy
Gibbons</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Ben_Harper?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Ben
Harper">Ben
Harper</a>,
and
O'Brien
himself
on
guitar.<sup
id="cite_ref-115"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-115"><span>[</span>115<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-116"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-116"><span>[</span>116<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>On
March
1,
2014,
Beck
was
the
musical
guest
on
a
<a
href="/wiki/Saturday_Night_Live?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Saturday
Night
Live">Saturday
Night
Live</a>
episode
hosted
by
<a
href="/wiki/Jim_Parsons?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Jim
Parsons">Jim
Parsons</a>.</p>

<script
type="text/javascript">




render_ads(false,
window['ad_config_bot']);





function
afc_match()
{








var
count
=
-1;








if(window['ad_config_top'])
{












count
=
window['ad_config_top'];








}









var
countBottom
=
0;








if(window['ad_config_bot'])
{












countBottom
=
window['ad_config_bot'];








}









if(window['backfillParam'])
{




























window['backfillParam']['pl_bmodn']
=
5;
























window['backfillParam']['pl_tnum']
=
count;












window['backfillParam']['pl_bnum']
=
countBottom;








}


































var
_matchUrl
=
"/afc-match?q=Beck&page=1&ac=24&qid=1ADD9B1733F3D25C52EFD242DA22862C&qsrc=121&dm=&qrt=2&lid="+
"&o=0&l=dir&oo=&cl=ca-aj-cat&ch=cx_ask_wiki,ad_dirN";





















_matchUrl+=
"&userip=76.78.3.114";




































_matchUrl+="&losid=a&locid=encw&lodid=us&loaid=a16";









var
location
=
window.location
+
"";








location
=
location.substring(7);








var
cutIdx
=
location.indexOf("/");








if
(location.indexOf(":")
>
-1)
{




















cutIdx
=
1
+
cutIdx
+
location.substring(cutIdx+1).indexOf("/");








}









var
urlPrefix
=
location.substring(0,
cutIdx);








_matchUrl
=
"http://"
+
urlPrefix
+
_matchUrl
+
"&afcec="
+
count
+
"&afcecb="
+
countBottom;








ajax_get(_matchUrl,
null,
null);




}





function
getXHR()
{








if
(window.XMLHttpRequest)
{












return
new
XMLHttpRequest();








}
else
if
(window.ActiveXObject)
{












try
{
















return
new
ActiveXObject("Msxml2.XMLHTTP");












}
catch
(e)
{
















try
{




















return
new
ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
















}
catch
(E)
{




















return
null;
















}












}








}








else
{












return
null;








}




}





function
ajax_get(url,
onsuccess,
onerror)
{








var
obj
=
getXHR();








if(obj)
{












obj.onreadystatechange
=
function()
{
















if(obj.readyState==4)
{




















if
(obj.status
==
200
&&
typeof(onsuccess)
==
"function")
{
























onsuccess(obj);




















}
else
if
(typeof(onerror)
==
"function")
{
























onerror(obj);




















}






















try
{
























delete
obj['onreadystatechange'];




















}
catch(e)
{}
















}












};












obj.open("GET",
url,
true,
"",
"");












obj.send(null);












return
obj;








}
else
{












if(onerror)
{
















onerror("Error
creating
XHR");












}
else
{
















a10.debug("Error
creating
XHR");












}












return
null;








}




}





afc_match();

</script>

<h2

<p
class="ur">
<span
class="grey
b

<span
class="qna-txt">
Glenn
Beck
is
a

and

<script
type="text/javascript"
src="/st/c/js/ask_unified-846e61d9870534b40a64bd4c1252bf1d0f50c43f.js"></script>



<script
type="text/javascript">








var
ask
=
ask
||
{};









(function(){












var
_timedOut
=
false,
















_fullPayload
=
window.backfillParam
||
{},
















_timeFromSerpStart
=
null,
































_adsLoggingTimeout
=
null,
















_dynamicLoggingTimeout
=
null;



























try{
















_timeFromSerpStart
=
((new
Date()
-
ask.CSA.startTime)
-
ask.CSA.showSerpStartTime);
































_adsLoggingTimeout
=
parseInt('2000')
-
_timeFromSerpStart;
















_dynamicLoggingTimeout
=
Math.max(_adsLoggingTimeout,
1);












}catch(e){
































_dynamicLoggingTimeout
=
2000;












}













function
mixinCSAAdData(payload){
















var
externalData
=
{




















csaInfo:
{
















































domTime:
ask.CSA.domReadyTime
?
ask.CSA.domReadyTime
:
0,
















































adsResponseTime:
ask.CSA.responseTime
?
ask.CSA.responseTime
:
0,
















































adsShownTime:
ask.CSA.adsShownTime
?
ask.CSA.adsShownTime
:
0,
















































serpShownTime:
ask.CSA.serpShownTime
?
ask.CSA.serpShownTime
:
0,
















































supplement:
_timedOut,
















































serpTimedOut:
!!ask.CSA.showSerpTimeoutFired,
















































serpTimeoutStartTime:
ask.CSA.showSerpStartTime
?
ask.CSA.showSerpStartTime
:
0,
















































dynamicTimeout:
_dynamicLoggingTimeout




















}
















};
















payload.pl_time
=
ask.CSA.responseTime
?
ask.CSA.responseTime
:
0;
















payload.pl_tnum
=
ask.CSA.numTopAds
?
ask.CSA.numTopAds
:
0;
















payload.pl_bnum
=
ask.CSA.numBottomAds
?
ask.CSA.numBottomAds
:
0;
















payload.pl_rnum
=
parseInt(payload.pl_tnum)
+
parseInt(payload.pl_bnum);
















try{




















payload.pl_edata
=
JSON.stringify(externalData);
















}catch(e){




































}












}














if
(ask
&&
ask.CSA)
{
















ask.CSA.addCSALoadCallback(function(){




























































var
payload
=
_timedOut
?
{
pl_supplement:
true
}
:
_fullPayload;





















mixinCSAAdData(payload);





















logBackfillEvent(payload);
















},
function(){








































_timedOut
=
